45b19(phal chen): gcig tu gnas pa yang ma yin te/ gnas pa dang / yongs su gnas pa yang rab tu ston to// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po yang ring du gnas pa yang
45b20(phal chen): ma yin/ yud tsam gcig tu gnas pa yang ma yin te/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la gnas pa dang yongs su gnas pa'ang rab tu ston to// 'di lta sde dper na nam mkha'
45b21(phal chen): ni kun nas nyon mongs pas nyon mongs par gyur pa'ang med la/ rnam par byang bas rnam par byang bar gyur pa'ang med do// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa'
45b22(phal chen): chen po yang 'jig rten la 'jug pas bsgribs pa yang med/ rnam par dag cing gsal bar gyur pa yang med do// 'di lta sde dper na nam mkha' ni 'jig rten thams cad kyi
45b23(phal chen): mngon sum du gyur pa yin te/ 'jig rten thams cad ni nam mkha'i mngon sum du gyur pa ma yin no// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po yang chos
45b24(phal chen): cad la mngon sum du gyur pa ste/ byang chub sems dpa' ni chos thams cad kyi mngon sum du gyur pa ma yin no// 'di lta ste dper na nam mkha' ni gnas thams cad/
46a1(phal chen): la rab tu gzhol ba yin te/ nam mkha'i mtha' ni yod pa ma yin no// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sem dpa' chen po yang chos kyi gnas
46a2(phal chen): thams cad la gnas te/ byang chub kyi sems ni mtha' yod pa ma yin no// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni bdag nyid nam mkha' dang mnyam par byas te/ yongs su bsgoms pa
46a3(phal chen): dang / rnam par sbyangs pa dang / shin du bsgrubs pa dang / mjam pa nyid du byas pa dang / rgyud kyi tshul gcig tu byas pa dang / ro gcig tu byas pa dang / tshad gcig tu byas pa
46a4(phal chen): nam mkha' lnga bur dag pa'i kha dog tu byas pa dang / thams cad du 'gro bar byas pa'i phyir ro// chos thams cad la yang dag par sems dpa' dang / khong du chud par byed pa dang /
46a5(phal chen): chos thams cad tha mi dad par rab tu 'thob par byed pa dang / zhing thams cad du 'gro bar bsgrubs pa dang / lus thams cad la gnas pa med pa yongs su rdzogs par byed pa dang /
46a6(phal chen): phyogs thams cad la rmongs pa med pa khong du chud bar byed pa dang / stobs thams cad tha mi dang bar sgrub pa dang / yon tan thams cad yul mtha' yas par yongs su rdzogs par byed
46a7(phal chen): pa dang / chos thams cad kyi 'byung gnas rab tu thob par byed pa dang / dpag du med pa thob par byed pa dang / rdo rje la du brtan pa la rab tu ga nol ba dang / dbyangs kyi lag chad med pa
46a8(phal chen): thams cad mngon par bsgrub pa dang / 'jig rten thams cad du byin cing chos kyi 'khor lo yongs su mi gtong ba'i phyir ro// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di ni byang chub sems dpa'
46b1(phal chen): tshul du 'gro ba med 'a
46b2(phal chen): sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi nam mkha' lta bu'i bzod pa thob pa ste bcu pa'o// bzod pa de dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni 'gro ba med pa'i lus rab tu
46b3(phal chen): 'thob bo// 'gag pa med pa'i tshul du skyes pa meng pa'i lus rab tu 'thob bo// 'jig pa med pa'i tshul du 'pho ba med pa'i lus rab tu 'thob po// ji ltar mthong ba ma yin pa'i tshul
46b4(phal chen): du bden pa med pa'i lus rab tu 'thob po// mtshan nyid med pa'i tshul du mtshan nyid gcig pa'i lus rab tu 'thob po// sangs rgyas kyi stobs chad med pa'i tshul du chad med pa'i lus
46b5(phal chen): rab tu 'thob po// de bzhin nyid kyi mtshan nyid kyi tshul du mnyam pa nyid kyi lus rab tu 'thob bo// dus gsum mnyam pa nyid khong du chud cing bzod pa'i tshul du tha mi dad pa'i lus rab tu
46b6(phal chen): 'thob bo// mnyam pa nyid kyi mig rnam par dag pas bsgribs pa med pa'i tshul du thams cad du 'gro ba'i lus rab tu 'thob po// chos thams cad dang ldan pa dang mi ldan pa med pa'i tshul
46b7(phal chen): tu 'dod chags dang bral ba'i mtha'i lus rab tu 'thob bo// bsod nams zad mi shes pa'i tshul du nam mkha' lngar mtha' dang dbus med pa rab tu 'thob bo// chos thams cad nam
46b8(phal chen): mkha'i rang bzhin gyi mtshan nyid kyis mtshan nyid gcig pa'i tshul du chos nyid mtsham pa nyid thob pas zad mi shes shing / thogs pa med pa rab tu 'thob bo// nam mkha' ltar
46b9(phal chen): thogs pa med pa'i tshul du dbyangs mtha' mas shing chang med pa rab du thob bo// nam mkha' ltar thams cad la thogs pa med pa'i tshul du byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa
47a1(phal chen): cad la mkhas pas yongs su rdzogs shing rnam par dag pa rab tu 'thob bo// nam mkha' ldar rgyun chad pa med pa'i tshul du sangs rgyas kyi chos rgya
47a2(phal chen): mcho gcig nas gcig du brgyud pa tshad med pa thams cad rab tu 'thob po// nam mkha' lngar tshad med cing mthar thug pa med pa'i tshul du sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad chad
47a3(phal chen): med pa'i zhing du byin gyis rlob pa rab tu 'thob bo// nam mkha' rgya mtsho'i tshul du chos thams cad kyi rnam par 'phrul pa rgyun mi 'chad par yang dag par ston pa yang yongs su
47a4(phal chen): rdzogs par 'gyur ro// nam mkha' ltar 'jig rten thams cad 'dzin pa'i tshul du lus thams cad 'jig pa med cing shin tu brtan pa yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ro//
47a5(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi gdung ba thams cad kyis nam mkha' rig par mi 'gyur ba'i tshul du rdo rje lta sra zhing brtan la rno ba'i dbang po yongs su 'grub par 'gyur ro// nam
47a6(phal chen): lnga bu'i ye shes kyi byin gyi rlabs kyi tshul du 'jig rten thams cad rab tu 'dzin pa'i stobs la yang dag par 'byung ngo // kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di dag ni byang chub
47a7(phal chen): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi bzod pa 'thob pa bcu pa'o// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun tu bzang pos don 'di nying
47a8(phal chen): bas kyang gsal bar bstan pa'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa'ang dag la tshigs su bcad ngede smras pa/ dzaM ltar skyes bral la zhig/ rin can 'byung gnas thos rgya
47b1(phal chen): nor tshogs chen po brtsegs don du// rab tu dga' ba skye ba yin// de bzhin shes rab che ldan pa'i// byang chub sems dpa' rgyal sras rnams// de bzhin gshegs pa'i
47b2(phal chen): chos kyi mtshan// zab cing zhi ba rab tu nyan// zab pa'i chos ni thos gyur cing // de dag yid ni 'jigs mi 'gyur// de dag sems la sdang ba med// skrag pa skye bar mi
47b3(phal chen): 'gyur ro// rgya chen dbyangs ni thos gyur nas// bzod pa'i dbyangs kyis byang chub tu// shes rab chen po yang dag 'jug/ de la the tsom skye ba med// bdag ni thams ca
47b4(phal chen): mkhyen par bya// bdag ni mi yi mgon tu bya// chos rab shin tu zab pa rnams// bdag gis sgra yi sgo nas thos// sku yi rjes su 'brang bas ni// dga' ba'i dam pa mi
47b5(phal chen): 'thob ces// de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos don du// de yi mos pa brtan pa skye// bsam pa byang chub sems rab kyis// 'dul zhing yongs su sgom par byed// chos
47b6(phal chen): rnams 'khrug par mi byed de// de yi dang ba rnam par 'phel// des ni swa rjes 'gro ba yi// bzod pa rab tu 'thob par 'gyur// spyod la shin tu brtson byed cing // dbya
47b7(phal chen): kyis bzod la rab tu gnas// chos kyi 'byung gnas yin pas na// shin du brtson par rab tu tshol// brtson 'grus ldog par mi byed de// sangs rgyas byang chub
47b8(phal chen): sgrib byed de// dbyangs tsam gyis ni gnas byed pas// byang chub sems la bag cha med// dbyangs kyi sa mos pa rab tu 'thob// des ni rgyas pa mnyes par byed/
48a1(phal chen): skyes bu la la bsod nams rgyas gyur pas// gser gyi 'byung gnas chen po rnyed gyur nas// brgyan pa'i gnas kyi rgyan tu rab sbyangs nas// de dag
48a2(phal chen): lus dang 'thun pa'i rgyan du byed// de bzhin mkhas pas chos kyi phul thos nas// sems dang blo yangs rgya mtshor bsgyur byas shing // ji ltar sngon thos chos rnams
48a3(phal chen): rtogs par byed// mi mthun tshul du chos la chos mi byed// de dag rtogs nas shin tu 'thun par spyod// rnam par mi sgom chos ni gang yang med// de dag chos
48a4(phal chen): rnams ci bzhin 'thun byed cing // de bzhin de ni chos rnams khong du chud par byed// khas pa'i sems ni rnam dag skyer 'gyur te// dga' ba'i sems yid rnams
48a5(phal chen): dang gsal ba skye// chos kyi yid la bdag nyid che ba brtson// rten cing 'brel 'byung chos la rab tu 'jug/ chos rnams mnyam pa nyid la de brtson te// dngos po
48a6(phal chen): rnam par bsgom la mngon par brtson// rgyal ba'i bzod dang dgal bar mi byed do// chos rnams mi mnyam med par rab tu shes// de ni bsam pa mthar thug rab
48a7(phal chen): brtan pas// rgyal ba'i byang chub ci bzhin rab tu spyod// ri rab bzhin du mi g.yo brtan pa yis// de'i bsam pa byang chub mchog la brten// mnyam bzhag sem
48a8(phal chen): dang ldan pas de brtson te// brtson 'grus ldan pa'i yid kyis rab tu spyod// bskal pa stong du sbyad pa spyod byed kyang // dor brtson 'grus 'jig par mi 'gyur ro//
48b1(phal chen): dag chos la yang dag de 'jug ste// rgyal ba'i rtogs bya'i gting yang rab tu rnyed// chos nyid zhi ba rab tu thob gyur pas// de la 'jug pa'i yid byed gang yang med// dpe ma/
48b2(phal chen): med pas 'di skad gsungs pa ltar// de ni chos rnams mnyam pa nyid du byed// mi mnyam tshul du bzod pa mi skyed de// ye shes mnyam nyid yongs su rdzogs par sgrub/
48b3(phal chen): bde bar gshegs pas 'thun par gang gsungs pa// de dag bzod pa'i sgo nas rab tu 'grub// chos rnams 'jig dang ldan pa ma yin te// chos nyid ci bzhin de 'dra
48b4(phal chen): tu shes/ lha gnas 'dri'i lha'i bu rnams 'dir 'dus dang // sum cu rtsa gsum gnas pa lnga rnams skyes gyur pa// de dag zil dang ra sna tshogs rnam pa gzhan dang gzhan//
48b5(phal chen): de dag khar ba'i snod gcig mngon spyod zar gyur na// zil dngar zhim pa de dag 'ongs pa ma yin te// phyogs bcu kun nas zil dngar stobs pa med// las rnams ji lnga ji bzhin
48b6(phal chen): lnga rnams de ltar za// de la skye ba med de bza' bar med pa yin// de bzhin byang chub sems dpa'i sems rab mngon skyes kyang // de la rdul cha'i chos kyang skyes par gyur pa med// ma skye
48b7(phal chen): gang yin chos de nam yang 'gag pa med// dam pa'i chos kyi rkyen rten mkhas pa rab tu zhugs/ ma 'gags gang yin mi zad chos rgyud de dang de// chos nyid 'di'i tshul la rab tu
48b8(phal chen): gnas pa yin// tha dad med pa'i chos dbyings 'di la rab tu 'jug/ 'jig rten tha dad med pa'i rgyud kyi tshul yang shes// de bzhin nyid mnyam 'jig rten zhi ba'i gnir gyur pa// gzhi
49a1(phal chen): med za dang med pa'i yang dag mtha' shes te// smon lam rdo rje'i rang bzhin 'grol ban phyir 'debs// rgyal sras de ni bde gshegs mkhyen la
49a2(phal chen): 'ang mngon chags med// de ni dben gzhol sangs rgyas chos rnams ston pa byed// chos kyi shugs las 'on kyang g.yo bar 'gyur ba med// brda dang grangs kyi tshul gyi
49a3(phal chen): mngon par 'du byed de// 'jig rten snying rtser smon lam dam pa rab tu 'debs// smon lam 'debs la gnas kyang stobs bcu ldan pa ste// 'gro ba ma lus kun la de
49a4(phal chen): ni gnas pa med// mkhas pa'i ye shes yongs su len dang 'dor ba spangs// chos dang chos kyi man ngag rnam pa'i tshul mkhas pa// 'di ni bzod pa'i dam pa ma
49a5(phal chen): skyes chos can te// des ni chos rnams zad med zad par mi 'gyur ro// mi skye'i tshul gyis yongs su bdams bya'i chos kyi dbyings// de bzhin nyid las brtan pa
49a6(phal chen): rnam par 'gyur ba med// rgyal sras byang chub don tu bzod pa 'di gnas pa// de la phyogs kun sangs rgyas mtha' yas lung ston to// rgyal sras de la sangs rgyas
49a7(phal chen): mkhyen pas dbang bskur mdzad// phyogs bcu kun nas rab tu snang bar mngon du gnas// de dag chos kun rab zhi rtag tu ni ba'i sems// mngon par sgrub cing da/
49a8(phal chen): ba kun la 'gro ba 'god// dus gsum chos rnams kun gyi mtshan ni dnge 'drabs// mtshan rnams yongs su dag byas sems can 'dul ba byed// sgyu ma lda du/
49b1(phal chen): chos rnams nges par sus rtogs pa// de dag 'jig rten sna tshogs du ma rtogs byed cing // 'jig rten sna tshogs sku tshul yang dag rtogs byas nas// las yangs
49b2(phal chen): shin tu bsags pas rnam pa sna tshogs pa// sems las las kyi rnam pa du ma 'byung 'gyur ro// de bas 'jig rten sems de sgyu ma lta bur bstan// de dag rnam
49b3(phal chen): brtags sgyu ma 'dra bas nus par 'gyur// srid pa'i lam rgyud ma was rgya 'dra yang dag man// ji ldar sgyu ma'i rnam pa byin rlabs byas pa'i gzugs// lam gyi
49b4(phal chen): gni mdor 'jig rten phal gyi nang bstan pa// 'gro bas mthong na de la kun kyang mos pa skyed// sgyu mas 'jig rten las ni gang yang 'grub mi 'gyur// de bzhin 'dra/
49b5(phal chen): ba ji snyed gang rnams yod pa dag/ sgyu ma'i rang bzhin lta bu ma skyes chos nyid de// dngos yod dngos med de bzhin yod dang med pa dang // skal ba mi mnyam tshul gyi//
49b6(phal chen): 'gro rgyung rab tu ston// sgyu ma'i tshul rnams shes nas sems can yongs su 'grel// sgyu ma lta bur yin par sems can khong du chud// sems can sgyu 'drang bzhin
49b7(phal chen): sgyu ma sems can 'dra// sems can med cing sgyu ma 'dra bar 'jig rten shes// sems can ning dang chos dang de bzhin dus gsum dang // 'jig rter thams cad
49b8(phal chen): ma'i rnam par rab tu 'byed// sgyu ma'i rnam pa lta bur chos rnams rab rtogs pas// 'jig rten ma lus 'di dag sgyu ma'i rnam par shes// skyes pa dag dang de bsgo//
50a1(phal chen): bud med rogs pa dang // bu mo de bzhin rnam par dul ba nye bar ston// glang po rnga dang ba lang phyugs dang shing rnams dang // me tog
50a2(phal chen): 'bras bu bzang dang ldan pa'i mtsho yang ston// thabs kyi rnam pa sna tshogs mang bar sgyu ma'i sems// sna tshogs gnas la'ang sgyu ma yongs su gnas pa med//
50a3(phal chen): sgyu ma dben la gnol zhing shing tu zhi ba yang // 'jig rten rnam par rtog pa sna tshogs mang po ston// de bzhin rgyal sras btsun pa rigs dang ldan pa rnams//
50a4(phal chen): rten sgyu ma sna tshogs ji bzhin ston par byed// sgom dang rnam par sgom pa'i dngos po'i sems kyang med// dngos po dngos med sgyu ma ji bzhin rab tu shes//
50a5(phal chen): zhing dang sems can chos kyi rnam pa mang por bcas// las rnams sna tshogs rnam pas yongs su bsags pa la// gnas par mi byed mngon par chags pa de
50a6(phal chen): bzhin med// chags med mtha'i sgyu ma'i tshul ni nges shes so// de ltar rgyal sras mkhas pa rnams// rab tu zhi la dga' zhing spros pa med pa ste// gnas med
50a7(phal chen): sa dang yang dag ldan// chos dbyings gnas pa de dag rab tu zhugs// de ni chos nyid rtogs pa ste// brtan pa de dag rgyal ba'i sku skyes sras yin no//
50a8(phal chen): 'du shes rgyu la mkhas pa ste// 'gro thams cad 'du shes 'dra bar shes// smig rgyu'i 'du shes 'dra ba ste// 'gro ba thams cad de ltar 'du shes phyin ci log/
50b1(phal chen): 'du shes rnam phye mkhas pa ste// de ni 'gro kun 'du shes spangs pa yin// sems can sna tshogs khong du chud// 'jig rten kun gyi sna tshogs rnam pa kun dang bral//
50b2(phal chen): 'jig rten 'du shes rab tu shes// 'jig rten 'du shes med min 'du shes ldan// phyogs rnams 'du shes dra ba ste// sems can mtha' yas 'du shes rnam pa sna
50b3(phal chen): tshogs yin// ma nor mig dang ldan pa rnams// 'jig rten sna tshogs 'du shes rab tu mthong // 'jig rten smig rgyu 'dra ba ste// 'du shes sna tshogs rnam pas 'dzin
50b4(phal chen): rten rnam par bkod// 'jig rten 'du shes gnas pa ste// de dgra phyin ci log gsum rnam par spangs// ji lngar smig rgyu'i tshogs kyi rnams// 'gro ba rnams
50b5(phal chen): la chu'i rnam pa dmigs pa snang // de la chu ni yong min yang // chu'i 'du shes rnam par rab tu slu// de bzhin 'jig rten thams cad kyang // khams gsum lam
50b6(phal chen): rgyur rnam pa sna tshogs mtha' yas te// 'du shes rnam pa smig rgyu bzhin// chags med yid ldan spyod yul mtha' yas so// 'du shes thams cad rnam par
50b7(phal chen): spang chags med ye shes ldan zhing spros pa med pa rnams// 'gro ba 'du shes chags gyur pa// 'du shes bslus las brtan pa 'grel par byed// nga rgyal/
50b8(phal chen): rlom dang dregs pa spangs// 'du shes thams cad bsal cing 'jig rten 'dren par byed// mi zang zad pa rtogs pa rnams// bden pa bang mi shes kyi tshul 'di/
51a1(phal chen): yin/ 'jig rten 'di dag thams cad rmi lam lta bur khong du chung // chos rnams thams cad rmi lam ngo bo nyid du rab tu rtogs// rmi lam de dag yul na mi
51a2(phal chen): gnas phyogs na'ang mi gnas te// rmi lam lta bur 'jig rjen rab tu ni la de dag gzhol// rmi lam rang bzhin mkhas shing rnam par rtog med chos dang ldan// rmi lam no//
51a3(phal chen): ba'i yid ldan sems la 'gyur ba gang yang med// 'jig rten kun tu rmi lam lta bu bshin du rgyu zhing spyod// dus gsum ma lus thams cad sgyu ma lta bu'i tshul du
51a4(phal chen): rtogs/ rmi lam 'i 'phor 'gyur ba med cing skye ba de bzhin med// rmi lam phyogs rnams kun na yod pa ma yin med pa min// khams gsum rmi lam lta bu'i 'di la
51a5(phal chen): rnam rtog med byas shing // rmi lam shin tu rdzogs mkhas de dag sems la bcings pa med// 'gro ba rmi lam rang bzhin 'dra la de dag mi gnas te// 'jig rten
51a6(phal chen): 'gro ba rnam par dben la de dag rten pa med// 'jig rten rnams la mi rtog de bzhin rnam par rtog pa med// rmi lam rtogs shing mkhas pa'i bzod pa'i sa ni 'di
51a7(phal chen): yin no// rmi lam 'gro ba rnams na rnam pa sna tshogs du ma snang // tha dang rnam pa gzhan dang gzhan du bye brag rnam pa mang // de bzhin ye shes zla bas 'gro ba tham
51a8(phal chen): cad rnam par mthong // rmi lam skra dang 'dra bar de dag rnam par rtog pa med// rmi lam lta bu'i tshul gyi rnam par brtan pas rab tu rtogs// de dag rmi lam mtshan/
51b1(phal chen): nying rnam 'das skal ba mnam pa min// rmi lam de dag gcig pa ma yin nam yang mang ba min// rmi lam rnam bkod rnam par 'gro ba thams cad rab tu shes/
51b2(phal chen): de dag sems nar thams cad rmi lam 'dra ba'i chos can dang // zhing rnams thams cad mi 'dra de bzhin chos rnams mi 'dra kun// ji ltar nyon mongs de bzhin rnam par byang ba
51b3(phal chen): du shes// 'jig rten rmi lam 'dra rnam par rtog par byed pa gang yang med// rmi lam lnga bur spyod pas yang ngag grub par gyur pa rnams// rmi lam lta bu'i smon lam rnam
51b4(phal chen): pas gnas pa med pa dag/ rmi lam lta bu'i chos rnams kun la gnas 'cha' mi byed de// 'jig rten rmi lam 'dral khyad par byed pa gang yang med// 'jig rten 'di
51b5(phal chen): dag rmi lam lnga bur byung bar shes shing dag/ rmi lam tshul rtogs 'gro ba kun tu mi 'jigs chos dang ldan// rmi lam bzhir spyod ldan pas 'jig rten kun tu chud mi za//
51b6(phal chen): ring thung kun kyang rmi lam rgyud bzhin de dag rab tu shes// 'di ni rmi lam lta bu'i yid ldan rnams kyi bzod pa ste// rmi lam lta bus 'jig rten sems can rab tu 'dren pa
51b7(phal chen): byed/ sems can rnams kyi bsam pa rtogs byas chags med ye shes can// sems la bcings med 'gro ba khrag khrig yongs su 'grel par byed// de ltar byang chub
51b8(phal chen): sems dpa'i spyod pa rgya che mtha' yas pa// chos rnams mngon par bsgrub pa yangs pa khong du chud byed de// chos kyi chos nyid du ma'i tshul rnams khong du nges chung ngo //
52a1(phal chen): chos tshul rnam pa tha dang kun la chags pa'i sems kyang med// 'gro kun dbyangs kyi yan lag rnam pa ji snyed yod pa yang // de dag dbyangs
52a2(phal chen): sma snyan bzhin du khong du des chud de// slar brjod de dag nang na med par rab tu shes pa de// sgra rnams thams cad byi nang med par rab tu de shes pa'o// sgra sman ji
52a3(phal chen): lhar rnam pa sna tshogs sgra tshul grag pa ste// rnam rtog dbyangs dang 'dra yang rnam rtog med pa'i sgra yang yin// sla rnams rnam par sna tshugs thams cad de bzhin
52a4(phal chen): rab shes te// sbal mngon par chags med de bzhir rlom sems med do// sems can kun gyi gtso bo thams cad nges ni mthong gyur cing // 'jig rten mgon
52a5(phal chen): po chos rnams gsung zhing dbyangs kyi srog mdzad pas// mdo mang brjod du med pa rab tu gsung ning ston mdzad kyang // rgyal ba'i gsung dbyangs de la de ni gnas
52a6(phal chen): bar mi byed de// sba sman de dag ji ltar sna'i rnam par grag byed kyang // sgra sran rnam pa dag la sra rnams gang yang yod pa min// de ltar dbyangs kyi bye brag rjes 'azang

72b2(phal chen): ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rus las mi 'da' ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
72b3(phal chen): kyi sangs rgyas kyi yul dpe med cing bsam gyis mi khyab pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad ma lus par dkyil mo dkrung gcig
72b4(phal chen): gis rgyas par dgang ba dang / dus gcig tu sangs rgyas thams cad bstar ba dang / 'od zer gcig gis 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad snang bar bya/
72b5(phal chen): ba dang / sku gzugs gcig gis lus dang gcig gzugs thams cad yongs su bstan pa dang / gnas gcig ra bzhugs kyang 'jig rten gyi khams thams
72b6(phal chen): cad ma lus par byor pa'i skur 'gyur ba dang / ye shes gcig rtogs pas chos thams cad la sgribs pa med par 'gyur ba dang / thugs gcig bskyed
72b7(phal chen): pas chos kyi dbyings thams cad ma lus par rgyas 'gyengs pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi che ba nyid tshad med pa dang ldar pa'i gshegs thabs gcig
72b8(phal chen): gis de kho na nyid yang dag par bstan pa dang / dus gsum thams cad sangs rgyas kyi go 'bar
73a1(phal chen): rgyas par 'gengs pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad dang ma 'dres par bzhugs shing / 'das pa dang / mabyon pa dang / nga ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan
73a2(phal chen): 'as rnams dang/ mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis rgyud kyi tshul gcig pa ste/ kyerdul ba'ims bcu ba dzi gnas sa rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyisangs rgyas kyi yul ba rgya
73a3(phal chen): tshang bsam gyis mi khyab pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po ni dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs mngon par bsgrubs pa'i ye shes te/ bdug na
73a4(phal chen): 'jug pa med pa'i chos thams cad la 'jug pas smon lam mngon par bsgrub pa'i ye shes dang / lus med pa la lus mngon par bsgrub pa'i ye shes dang / chos thams cad mi gnyis
73a5(phal chen): pa la mngon par 'tshang rgya ba mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / sems can gyi mthar thug par bdag med pa la sems can 'dul ba mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / chos thams
73a6(phal chen): cad mtshan ma med pa la mtshan ma sna tshogs mngon par bslab pa'i ye shes dang / 'jig rten gyi khams kyi yul ma skyes pa la 'jig rten gyi khams 'dru ba dang 'jig pa mngon par
73a7(phal chen): bsgrub pa'i segs dang / thams cad mngon pa 'du bya ba med pa la/ las kyi rnam par sri pa mngon par bsgrub pa'i seshes dang / chas thams cad brjod du med pa
73a8(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings su gsung ma'in par bsgrub pa'i ye shes dang / chos thams cad kun nas tshan mongs pa dang / rnam par byang bas 'jug pa med pa la kun nas chen mangs
73b1(phal chen): pa dang / rnam par byang ba mngon par bsgrub pa'i mashes dang / chos thams cad ma skyes pa la skye ba dang / 'jig pa'i mtshan cing chen cing 'brel par 'byung ba la mngon par
73b2(phal chen): bsgrub pa'i ye shes te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras pa'i bcu po de dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi mngon sangs rgyas kyi mngon par bsgrub pa'i ye shes so// kye rgyal ba'i sras
73b3(phal chen): bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshad med pa'i khongs chud pa dag ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi sku ni dus gsum thams cad
73b4(phal chen): kyi rjes su 'brang ba'i khongs su chung ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can thams cad 'dul ba mdzad pa ni cho 'phrul chen po gsum gyi khongs su chung ba yin/
73b5(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams tshig rab cu dbye ba thams cad las mkhas pa ni sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi chos kyi gsungs thams cad kyi khongs su chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas @
73b6(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi rna rnams kyi chos kyi 'khor lo thams cad ni de bzhin gshegs pa tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa bzhir khongs su chud ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom
73b7(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams sems can thams cad yongs su mi gtong ba ni thugs rje chen po khongs su chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams rtags du mnyam par dag
73b8(phal chen): pa nongs thams cad dusems can thams cad la rnam par gzims pa'i khongs su chung pa man/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis sangs rgyas kyis ngag dza
74a1(phal chen): ba mamasas rnam pa 'phral brnams la langs su chud pa las/ sangs rgyas ba rnam pan+d+ha@
74a2(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings thams cad khangs su chung ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis skad rtsig bcig tan 'das pa rang ma byur ba dang lngar byung ba'i sangs
74a3(phal chen): rgyas skye ba thams cad khongs su chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi ma macig du ni dus gsum gyi brgal ba'i grangs khong du chung par bstan pan+d+han+d+ha
74a4(phal chen): 'ang du drung ba yin/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu ba dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rkang med pa'i 'angs su chung ba'o// kye rgyal po'i sras bcum
74a5(phal chen): dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba rnams kyi chang med pa'i khongs sar+b+ba pa la// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcus
74a6(phal chen): 'di dag bcug rnam bdud byed du mas ma rab tu 'joms 'ang rnams par 'brang ba nisangs rgyas bcob ldan 'das rnams kyi shin du rgya po ma ca pa
74a7(phal chen): 'o/ mu segs can gzhan darnams kyi rgol bcar bcang ba na sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi na ba tsham bzod par dka' ba'o// 'dul ba'i sems
74b1(phal chen): chen gyi khams thams cad du gshegs pa ni du sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka'o// chos kyi dbyings thugs su chud pa'i ye shes ni sangs
74b2(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin du rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o// 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad ma lus par skus khyab cing / sangs rgyas kyi sku rnams par phye ba sna
74b3(phal chen): tshogs thams cad dumi gnyis pa sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin du rgyuche ba'i chos bzod par na/ gsung gi san la gathams canam sems carnams par byab
74b4(phal chen): dang / thob par bya ba dang / gdul bar bya ba don mong par so so yang dag par rig pa rdzogs pa med par bstan pa'i tshul du so so yang dag par rig pa bani 'byung ba ni/
74b5(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin du rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu ba su'i bu ga gcig nas/ de bzhin gshes
74b6(phal chen): pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed bsam gyis mi khyab cing / thogs pa med pa'i tshul du 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin du phra ba snyed kyis
74b7(phal chen): kyis 'byung zhing de bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi sku'i ba spu'i bu ga thams cad nas 'byung ba ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi shin du rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o// de bzhin/
74b8(phal chen): gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rdul shin du phra ba gcig la sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'jog rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin du phra ba snyed yongs
75a1(phal chen): su ston cing / sangs rgyas kyi rgyan dang rang bzhin gyi lngab lhub dang / chos kyi 'khor la bskor brgyan mi 'char cing sems can rnam par gdul bathogs pa
75a2(phal chen): med la/ 'jig rten gyi khams de dag tu gtogs pa rnams la'ang ma bang ba dang / gnad pa med kyang rdul na du ma pa rang mangs par ma byas/ 'jig rten gyi khams da
75a3(phal chen): kyang chung bar ma byas par ji ltar gnas pa'i rnam chos kyi dbyings kyang thugs su chung ba'i ye shes mnga' ba ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin du rgya che ba'i chos bzod par
75a4(phal chen): dka'o// mun pa med pa'i khams de bzhin gshegs pas mngon par sangs rgyas te/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la mun pa med cing bsgribs pa mi mnga' la/ sems can
75a5(phal chen): pha rol gyi spobs pa sna tshogs kyi gnas rnam par sel na/ de la bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu dang ldan pa ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
75a6(phal chen): shin du rgya che ba'i chos bzong bar dka' ba ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi na rgya che ba'i chos 'thod par dka' ba'o//
75a7(phal chen): rgyal ba'i sas 'dra ba 'di gnas sargyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kya gnyi ci rnam pa rnam bcad du banas mthamam ci shin du ga pan/ rnam
75a8(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi yang dag par bsgrub pa bdag tshad rgya ba ni sngon gyi mtha' nas rnam pa thams cad du banas mtho ba ma tshang rnam par dag 'a'o// sangs rgyas
75b1(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'das pa dang / mabyod pa dang / daltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas kyi chung ngu rigs dang ldan par 'byung ba'i bdag nyid che ba ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i
75b2(phal chen): tshigs rnam par dag pas rnam pa thams cad du kha nas mtha' med cing shin du rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rnam par shes pa la mi gnas pa
75b3(phal chen): / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ban phy-i 'i mtha'i zur thug par grangs pas rnam pa thams cad du 'anas maHba med ci shi tu nam par dag

75b7(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sngon gyi mtha' dang phyi ma'i mthar chos kyi dbyings la gnas pas mnyam pa'i bsod nams mi zad pa dang ldan pas mi zad pa'i bsod nams

76a1(phal chen): 'das rnams ni sku gzugs dang kha dog mtha' yas pas 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad na sems can 'dul ba'i dus dang dbang gis chags pa med par
76a2(phal chen): bzhugs par sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni rnam pa thams cad du khan ma tho ba med ci bzhin du rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das/

78a6(phal chen): 'di lta ste/ pha rol tu phyin pa thams cad kyis mngon par 'byung ba 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rgya rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di lta ste chos thams cad la mi
78a7(phal chen): mkhyen pa gang yang mi mang ba 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi tshul yin no// 'di lnga sde thams cad kyang thugs rjes chen po ldan pa 'dzam sangs rgyas
78a8(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di lta ste thams cad kyang stobs bcu tshang med pa dang ldan pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'a
78b1(phal chen): lha sde thams cad kyang bla na med pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bskor ba 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di lta sde thams cad kyang sems can 'dul ba

78b7(phal chen): sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos mtha' yas pa shin du bstan pa'i sgo rnams te/ gabacu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan
78b8(phal chen): 'das rnams ni sems kyi khams shin du bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can gyi saspyong pa sna tshogs shin du bstan pa'i sgor/
79a1(phal chen): mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can thams cad kyi las dang rnam par smin par shin du bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o/
79a2(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can thams cad la gdams ngag shin du bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can
79a3(phal chen): mtha' yas pa rnam par myong ba'i nan tan gyi sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad la gdams ngag
79a4(phal chen): dang man ngag gis yongs su gzhog pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i khyad par gyi smon lam rnam
79a5(phal chen): pa tha dad pas 'byung ba shin du bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas thabacom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad ma lus pa'i 'du ba dang
79a6(phal chen): 'jig pa shin du bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnam par dag pa ni byang chub sems dpa'i bsam
79a7(phal chen): ba dang mas pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa rnams cad du
79a8(phal chen): 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar 'byung ba'i sangs rgyas gcig nas gcig tu brgyud ba ni bskal pa yangs pa de dang de dag tu bstan cing brjod pa dang / yongs su bshan
79b1(phal chen): pas sangs rgyas kyis ye shes thams cad khong du chud par bya ba'i sgor mtha' yas pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu pa de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas
79b2(phal chen): kyi chos mtha' yas pa shin du bstan pa'i sgo'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las sems can rnams
79b3(phal chen): kyis sgrub pa ste/ bcu gang zhe ma/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku yongs su bstan pa ni sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las bslab pa'o// sangs rgyas
79b4(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gsung yang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las bsgrub pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams len pa mdzad pa yang sems can
79b5(phal chen): rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las sgrub pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams len pa mi mdzad pa yang / sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las sgrub
79b6(phal chen): pa'o// sa dang chu dang me dang rlung gis kyang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las sgrub pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
79b7(phal chen): rnams ni byin gyi brlabs kyi yul mnga' bas dmigs pa thams cad yul du mdzad pas kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las bslab po// sangs rgyas ba
79b8(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi mtshan kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las sgrub bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams mi nang la dmigs par mdza bas kyang
80a1(phal chen): sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las sgrub bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnam par dag pas kyang sems
80a2(phal chen): pa can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin sgrub po// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams mi gsungs par yang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las srub sa/
80a3(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las sems can rnams la bsgrub po// bam po drug bcu rtsa bzhi pa
80a4(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sems can gyi gtso bo chos te/ bcu gang zhe na/ smon lam
80a5(phal chen): chen po la rab tu brtan zhing smon pa lam zhig pa mi mnga' bas ji skad du gsungs pa de ltar mdzad cing gnyis su mi gsung ba 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos
80a6(phal chen): dang pa'o// phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thugs pa'i bskal pa thams cad du byang chub sems dpa'i myong ba la yon tan thams cad yongs su rdzogs par mdzad pas rab tu brtson
80a7(phal chen): zhing sgyid lug pa mi mnga' ba 'di ni sems can gyis gtso bo'i chos gnyis pa'o// sems can gdul bar 'gyur ba gcig cig gzigs kyang 'jig rten gyi khams
80a8(phal chen): 'arjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa gshegs cing / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad dru gshegs pa la thags thogs med pa 'dzini sems can gyimamatshan
80b1(phal chen): chos gsum pa'o// zhe sdang ba'i sems can rnams la thugs rje chen pos snyoms pa dang / ngang pa'i sems can rnams la thugs rje chen pos spoms pa'i ngani sems ca
80b2(phal chen): gtso bo'i chos bzhi pa'o// gang gi tshe ga bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yang dag par zhugs nas bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngo
80b3(phal chen): par sangs rgyas kyi bar du de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas su mi 'gyur ro snyam du byang chub kyi sems ma nyams pa'i byang chub tu
80b4(phal chen): mngon par sangs rgyas kyi bar 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos lnga pa'o// dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad yang dag par sgrub cing thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yongs su bsdu
80b5(phal chen): bas 'jug go// 'jig rten pa'i rgyud la ma yin pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos drug pa'o// sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rjes su sngon sangs rgyas kyis sapyad pa'i
80b6(phal chen): sems su lus kyi las dang ngag gi las dang yid kyi las kyis slob cing nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi spyod pas thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yongs su bsngo bas med pas
80b7(phal chen): bla na med pa yang dag par rdzoga'i ba'i byang chub tu mngon par sangs rgyas pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos bdun pa'o// byang chub sems dpa'i sems rnam par dag
80b8(phal chen): cing 'ong bsal la dad pa thams cad du snang zhing kun tu 'od 'byung ba/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la snang zhing thams cad du snyoms par thams cad mkhyen pa nyid
81a1(phal chen): yongs su rdzogs par byed pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso ba'i chos brgyad pa'o// 'jig rten pa'i bde ba thams cad yongs su spangs te/ 'jig rten pa'i
81a2(phal chen): dga' dga' ba thams cad la ma chags pa dang / 'jig rten thams cad gyis gos pa med pa'i smon lam thams cad du mnyam pa nyid kyis/ 'jig rten thams cad bde ba
81a3(phal chen): thams cad dang ldan par byas te/ sdug bsngal dang spros pa thams cad rab tu 'joms pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos dgu pa'o// sdug bsngal gyi mi ba batham
81a4(phal chen): cad nyams su bab ste/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi don du dka' thub gyis shin du gdungs kyang bla bar sems bskyed par pas sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rigs yongs su bsrung
81a5(phal chen): ba dang ldan pa dang / stobs bcu'i bar sa'i bar du sangs rgyas kyi yul la mos pas mthar thug pa 'drin sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos bcu pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras
81a6(phal chen): bcu po de dag na sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sems can gyim rgya ma chos so// kyi rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag mi sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyis
81a7(phal chen): rgyas kyi rnam par sbyong ba chags pa med pa rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jim rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du gshegs pas chas
81a8(phal chen): pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad na zhugs pas chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par byung
81b1(phal chen): pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad na zhugs pa dang bzhengs pa dang bzhud pas chags pa mi mnga' bar spyong ba yin/ sangs rgyas
81b2(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du chos ston pas chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
81b3(phal chen): ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad kyi dga' ldan gyi gnas na bzhugs kyang chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos/
81b4(phal chen): kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi sngon gyi mtha' dang phyi ma'i mtha' dang da ltar byung ba'i mtha' la chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
81b5(phal chen): rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad tsam gyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor na zhugs kyang chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par pyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
81b6(phal chen): rnams ni sems can ma lus pa thams cad kyi sems dang pyod pa la gzigs shing thugs kyi skad cig gcig la cho 'phrul chen po gsum gyis sems can rnam par 'dul yang
81b7(phal chen): chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par sbyong ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sku gcig gis kyang tshad med bsam gyis kyang mi khyab pa'i sangs rgyas kyi rnam par
81b8(phal chen): stong pa chen por rnam par spyod kyang chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par myong ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems kyis khams 'byam klas pa ma lus pa
82a1(phal chen): thams cad du de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos ma lus pa thams cad kyi mthar thug pa bsam gyis mi khyab par ston cing gsung yang chags pa mi mnga' bar
82a2(phal chen): rnam par spyod pa yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par myong ba chags pa meng pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i
82a3(phal chen): sum bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rgyan mchog ngam pa bla na med pa rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
82a4(phal chen): rnams kyi sku mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po sna tshogs kyis rnam par brgyan pa ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku'i rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas
82a5(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gsung yan lag gi mchog dam pa drug bcu dang ldan zhing yan lag lnga brgyas yongs su bzung ba dang / rgyun brgya stong du mas rab tu brgyan pa
82a6(phal chen): dang / dbyangs kyi yan las mtha' yas mu med pas rnam par dag pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi don dang tshig dang yi ge brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pas rab tu tshim
82a7(phal chen): par mdzad pa dang / bag cha ba mi mnga' bar seng ge'i nga ro chen po bzlog pa dang / 'jigs pa med pa chen pos bsnyengs pa mi mnga' bar gyur pa dang / chos kyi dbyings
82a8(phal chen): ma lus pa thams cad du sems can thams cad la thag cing gsal te khong du chud bar 'gyur ba dang / sems can bsam pa tha dad pa dang / dbang po tha dad pa rnam pa
82b1(phal chen): sna tshogs 'dul bar gnas pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gsung gi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thugs/
82b2(phal chen): kyi 'phrin las ni stobs bcus brgyan pa sangs rgyas kyi ting nge 'dzin chen po thams cad kyi me tog shin du rgyas pa/ sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad kyi rgyan gyis shin
82b3(phal chen): du brgyan cing bsgrub pas chags pa med pa'i spyod yul dang ldan pa/ chos kyi dbyings kyi bzhi la rab tu rten pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos gting med pa rab tu brnyes pa/
82b4(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi rgyan du gyur pa/ dus gsum gyi chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi sems can kun gyi sems dang myod pa thams cad skad cig
82b5(phal chen): gcig dang ldan pa'i shes rab kyis rab tu mkhyen pa ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thugs kyi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom
82b6(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams ni 'od zer bye ba brjod du med pa rab tu 'gyed pa mdzad de/ 'od zer de dag re re la yang 'od zer gyi dkyil 'khor gyi dra ba brjod du med pa dang ldan pa
82b7(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'byam klas pa thams cad ma lus par snang bar byed pa cing 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud thams cad munar pa med par ston pa/ sangs rgyas skye ba dang ma
82b8(phal chen): 'bral bas sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las las phyir mi ldog cing don yod pa sangs rgyas skye ba brjod du med pas gnas pa med pa/ rang bzhin rnam par dag cing kun
83a1(phal chen): snyoms par 'byung ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'od zer gyi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// gnas pa med pa/ sangs rgyas bcom/
83a2(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams bzhad mo 'jam par sbon na/ zhal gyi sgo nas 'od zer kha dog sna tshogs kha dog du ma dang ldan pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong brjod du med pa/ phyogs bcu'i
83a3(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus par thams cad snang bar byed pa/ sems can gyi khams tshad med grangs med bsam gyis mi khyab pa rnam par ston pa/ bla na med pa ya
83a4(phal chen): dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu rnam par gzhan du mi 'gyur bar lus lung ston pa 'gro ba thams cad du shin du gsal ba 'byung ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'a
83a5(phal chen): rnams kyi zhad mo 'dzum pa bstan pa'i rgyar mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi sku ni tshad med pa ste/ bsgribs pa
83a6(phal chen): med pas rnam par dag pa/ chos thams cad chags pa med pa nyid kyi mthar thug pa/ mtha' dang dbus med pa'i chos kyi dbyings la gnas pa/ 'jig rten thams can
83a7(phal chen): dang ma 'dzes pa/ 'jig rten thams cad dang 'ji ba med pa/ 'jig rten thams cad kyi de kho na nyid la yang dag par zhugs pa/ 'jig rnam thams cad las gyen du
83a8(phal chen): 'phags pa/ 'jig rten las 'das pa chos kyis yang dag par srung ba/ tshig gi lam dang bral ba/ brjod du med pa'i mthar phyin pa/ phung po dang khams pa/
83b1(phal chen): skye mched dang bral ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku'i rgya mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams na 'ad tshang med pa
83b2(phal chen): mnga' ba ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du 'ong ma 'dres shing lnga rgyan du ma dang ldan pa/ kha dog sna tshogs brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rgyan
83b3(phal chen): dang ldan pa/ 'od kyi snang ba kun du thogs pa med cing / thams cad du rtsegs pa med/ pa/ 'od kyi dkyil 'khor bsgribs pa med pa tshad med pa'i mdzod du gyur pa/ 'od
83b4(phal chen): thams cad kyi 'byung gnas su gyur pa ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni
83b5(phal chen): kha dog mtha' yas pa mnga' ba ste/ kha dog ming du 'ong ba mnga' ba'o// kha dog 'od gsal ba mnga'o// kha dog tshad med pa mnga' ba'o// sems can gyi khams ma
83b6(phal chen): lus pa thams cad kyi bsam pa dang mos pa bzhin du rngam par dmigs pa'i kha dog mnga' ba'o// de ma yin pa'i kha dog gzhan khams gsum du gtogs pa thams ca
83b7(phal chen): zil gyis gnon pa'i kha dog mnga' ba'o// kha dog thams cad kyi pha rol du phyin pa brnyes pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni kha dog bla na med pa mnga' ba ste/
83b8(phal chen): 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi kha dog gi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dge ba'i shin du rnam par dag
84a1(phal chen): paste/ 'das pa dang ma byon pa dang da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rigs dge ba'in po che'i 'byung gnas su gyur pa la shin du byung
84a2(phal chen): ba'o// chos nyid kyi rnam pa thams cad du khyad par yod pa dang / khyad par med pa'i pyod pas rnam par dag par dag pa'i rgyan gyis ye shes smra ba thams cad kyi nang
84a3(phal chen): du gtogs pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs bsgrib pa med pa'i rgyung rnam par dag pas 'jig rten gyi mi snyam pa thams cad kyis mi snyan par brjod du mang ba ste/ 'dzin
84a4(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rigs dang rgyud rnam par dag pa'i rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byas
84a5(phal chen): pa chen po'i mthu dang rang bzhin gyi rgyan mnga' ba ste/ shin du dang ba yongs su pA'i rnyog pa mnga' ba/ sku'i 'phrin las yongs su brtsal pa/ blta bas mi skyo ba thugs
84a6(phal chen): shin rnam par gsal ba/ thugs rje chen po mnga' ba/ 'gro rnams cad sgrub pa/ yon tan gyi gnas kyi dam pa bla na med pa/ yongs su 'dzin pa'i nangan rdzogs pa
84a7(phal chen): bcan phan par mabyung ba sems canathams cad kyi don du ye shes chen pa tsun gyis brlab ste/ bsod nams chen pos yongs su 'phags pa/ 'gro ba thams cad
84a8(phal chen): bas rnams kyi zhing du gyur pa/ sems can rnams kyi san na nga ma shes kyi phung po thams cad rnam par 'phel bar mdza pa ste/ 'dzin sangs rgyas bcom ldan
84b1(phal chen): 'das rnams kyi byams pa chen po dang / thugs rje chen po'i mthar thug pa bsod nams kyi rgyar mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sa
84b2(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi
84b3(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sgyur ba'i chos rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos thams cad la mnga' ba dang / chos thams
84b4(phal chen): cad la snang bar mdzad pa'i mnga' sgyur bas tshig dang yi ge mtha' yas pa la thogs pa mi mnga' ba'i spobs pa mnga' ba dang / chos thams cad ma lus par yongs su
84b5(phal chen): brjod pas mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sgyur ba'i chos dang po'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan
84b6(phal chen): 'das rnams ni sems can ji ltar yongs su smin pa dang / smon lam ji ltar btab pa'i tshul bzhin du 'dul ba la thogs pa mi mnga' bas/ mnga' che ba ste/ 'dzi
84b7(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sgyur ba'i chos gnyis pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad sems can gcig
84b8(phal chen): la'ang gnod pa med par rnam pa drug tu rab tu spyod pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams rgyan rnam par bkod pa grangs med tshad med pa dang ldan pa/ nam mkha'i dbyings kyi/
85a1(phal chen): mthas gtugs pa thams cad gcig nas gcig tu 'bang ba dang / gcig nas gcig tu bcug pa dang / gcig nas gcig tu bzlab dang / gcig nas gcig tu ba sa
85a2(phal chen): bas/ 'jig rten gyi khams gzhan gyi phyogs su rab tu bzhag kyang sems can gyi khams rnams 'khor cing / rmongs par mi 'gyur la/ the tsom du mi 'gyur bar mdzad pas mnga' che ba
85a3(phal chen): ste/ 'jig 'di ni sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sbyar ba'i chos gsum pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad byin gyis
85a4(phal chen): brlob pa'i ye shes kyis 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyun phan tshun du byin gyis brlab pa dang / thugs skad cig gcig gis 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rgyan yang dag par bstan pa
85a5(phal chen): pa dang / bskal pa grangs med par brjod kyang ye shes yi ge shin du bstan pa zang mi shes pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad rgyan thams cad kyis rnam par brgyan pa
85a6(phal chen): mi mthun pa med cing nye bar tsho mongs pa med pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi ning gcig tu yongs su 'dra ba sangs rgyas kyi ning rnam par dag pa thams cad byin gyis brlab pa la mnga' cheb sa/
85a7(phal chen): 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnabs kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sbyar ba'i chos bzhi pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyis 'dul ba'i
85a8(phal chen): sems can gzigs na/ sems can gcig gi don du bskal pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med par skyil mo krung gcig gis bzhugs na yang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i skul
85b1(phal chen): mi bde ba mi mnga' zhing thugs la mi bde ba mi mnga' ste/ gang zag re yang mi bslebs 'dul ba'i dus las mi 'da' ba dang / gang zag gcig la ci lta ba de bzhin du rim par 'jig
85b2(phal chen): rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i sku tshel mnga' bar byin gyis brlabs te/ bzhugs kyang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams la skyo ba mi mnga' ba
85b3(phal chen): ste/ de ltar sems can gyi khams thams cad mthar gyis rim pas sangs rgyas kyis 'dul ba'i gang zag gi don du yongs su skyong ba mdzad pa la mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom
85b4(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sgyur ba'i chos lnga pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du yang dag par gzhol ba'i
85b5(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa'i gzhung pas 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du bzhud pa la thags thogs mi mnga' ba dang / phyogs bcu'i chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi 'jig rten
85b6(phal chen): gyi khams kyi rgyud rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa dang / phyogs kyi dra ba'i rgyud thams cad du zhugs skad cig gcig dang ldan pas bzhud par byin gyis rlob cing chos kyi dbyings shin du bstan pa khong
85b7(phal chen): du chud par bya bas chos kyi 'khor lo thogs pa med pa rab tu bskor ba la mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sbyar ba'i chos
85b8(phal chen): drug pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'dul ba'i sems can gyi khams thams cad kyi don du thugs skad cig re re la bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub
86a1(phal chen): tu mngon par 'chad par mnga' che ba ste/ de la chos thams cad mngon par sangs rgyas pa'ang gang yang med la/ mngon par sangs rgyas pa med de/ mngon par
86a2(phal chen): 'tshang rgya bar 'gyur ba med kyang slob pa'i sa la gnas shing mngon par 'tshang rgya bar yang mi brjod par dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad kyang bsgribs pa med par rtogs
86a3(phal chen): par thugs su chud pas sems can thams cad gdul ba'i don du ye shes tshad med pa'i tshul gyis sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa chen po'i yul yongs su rgyun mi gcod pa 'din
86a4(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sgyur ba'i chos bdun pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni spyan gyi skye mched kyis sangs
86a5(phal chen): rgyas kyi 'dzin las ga bsgrubs pa de snyan gyi skye mched kyis yongs su 'grub par mdzad do// sran gyi skye mched kyis sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las gang bsgrub pa de/ shangs
86a6(phal chen): skye mched kyis yongs su 'grub par mdzad do// gangs kyi skye mched kyis sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las gang bsgrub pa re/ ljags kyi skye mched kyis yongs su grub pa mdzad do//
86a7(phal chen): ljags kyi skye mched kyis sangs rgyas kyi 'phyir las gang bsgrub pa de ni/ sku'i skye mched kyis yongs su grub par mdzad do// skye su'i skye mched kyis sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin la
86a8(phal chen): gang bsgrub pa'i thugs kyi skye mched kyis yongs su grub par mdzad do// thugs kyi skye mched kyis sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las gang bsgrub pa de 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus
86b1(phal chen): ma su yu /
86b2(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams mi rang gi sgo'i baspu'i khrug gcig gi nang du sems can gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad gzung bar mdza coM posangs sa rlang pa ma
86b3(phal chen): dang / sems can ri zhing yang lus sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du ma pa tsam chu yangs par mdzad kyang sems cad de dag la gnod pa dang / mi bde bar mi 'gyur ba dang /
86b4(phal chen): tu yang sems can re re zhing 'jig rten gyi khams gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pas bskal pa grangs med pa zang par gnas par bya ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams grangs med
86b5(phal chen): par gom pa gcig gis phyin pas/ 'jig rten gyi khams de dag tu sangs 'byung ba rnams kyi spyan sngar 'gro bar bya ba dang / sangs rgyas de dag 'byung ba'i tshe/ yang brjod du/
86b6(phal chen): med pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud dang gling de dag na sems can gyi gtso bos brjod du med pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bar bya ba dang / ba spu'i bu ga de na sangs rgyas
86b7(phal chen): gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa 'byung bar bya ba dang / sems can gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa brjod du med pa 'byung bar bya ba dang /
86b8(phal chen): chos kyi 'khor lo gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa bskor bar bya ba dang / chos kyi dbyings bstan pa gnas gcig tu brgyud pa brjod du med
87a1(phal chen): / pa'i yang brjod du med pa shin du bstan par bya ba dang / 'das pa gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa brjod du med pa dang / ma 'ongs pa gcig nas gcig tu rgyud
87a2(phal chen): pa brjod du med pa dang / da ltar byung ba gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa brjod du med pa yongs su brjod par bya ba dang / nam mkha'i dbyings mtha' dang dbus med par
87a3(phal chen): bstan pa kun du mtshams med par sems can thams cad 'ong zhing 'gro ba dang / skye ba'i skye mched thams cad du 'dod pa'i longs spyong rgya chen po bgegs med pa thams
87a4(phal chen): cad du 'byung bar bya ba la mnga' che ba ste 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sgyur ba'i chos dgu pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom
87a5(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad du pad+mo'i rgyan chen pos brgyan pa'i seng ge'i khri pad+mo'i snying po can la de bzhin gshegs pa gcig gi chos
87a6(phal chen): kyi dbyings tshad med pa thams cad du khyab pa'i sgras byang chub mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas te/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa thams cad yongs su bstan
87a7(phal chen): pa mdzad pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa gcig gi ji lta bar 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin du phra ba snyed kyi sems can gyi matsob thams cad kyang / de bzhin
87a8(phal chen): du dgongs pa skad cig ma re re'i byin gyis brlabs kyis brlabs pa dang / dgongs pa skad cig la ji lta ba bzhin du dgongs pa skad cig ma thams cad la'ang pad+mo'i rgyur/
87b1(phal chen): kyis sangs su ngas par mngon par 'chang rgya bar bya ba dang / de bzhin du chos kyi dbyings thams cad ma lus pa'i sangs rgyas kyi ning brjod du med pa rnam par dag pa/ rgya tsha/
87b2(phal chen): dang ldan pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams su dmigs pa rnam pa sna tshogs dang ldan pa'i zhing rnam par dag pa 'byam klas pa brjod du med pa/ mtshan nyid tha dad pa rnam pa thang
87b3(phal chen): pa'i rgyud tshad med cing 'byam klas pa/ dus kyi rgyud kyi grangs med pa dang ldan pa/ bstan pa ma 'dres pa dang ldan pa/ blo tshad med pa dang / mos pa shin du yangs pa
87b4(phal chen): dang ldan pa/ mtshan nyid sna tshogs kyi gnas med pa/ mtshan nyid bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang ldan pa/ tshad med pa thams cad dgongs pa/ skad cig ma las dgongs pa/
87b5(phal chen): skad cig ma gcig gis thams cad yongs su bstan kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams skye mched du sgrub pa mi mdzad pa la mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas btsa
87b6(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sgyur ba'i chos bcu pa skye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi
87b7(phal chen): mnga' chen po sbyar ba'i chos so// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos yongs su rdzogs pa tshad med pa
87b8(phal chen): bsam gyis mi khyab pa rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ mtshan re re zhing bsod nams kyi sangs rgyas yongs su dag par 'gyur ba 'di ni yongs su rdzogs pa dang po ste/
88a1(phal chen): des sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'cha brgya'o// sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams yongs su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'a
88a2(phal chen): rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad yongs su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'chang rgya'o// ma
88a3(phal chen): tan thams cad kyi 'byung gnas su phun sum tshogs pa'i spyong pa yongs su dag pa yongs su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang
88a4(phal chen): rgyu'o// sems can yongs su rdzog smin par bya ba dang / gdul ba yongs su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// sangs rgyas
88a5(phal chen): kyi mnga' 'gro ba thams cad kyis zil gyis mi non pa'i yongs su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// zhing yongs su dag
88a6(phal chen): par bya ba yongs su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes yongs su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas
88a7(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'chang rgya'i// mtshan par dang pe byang bzang po dang gzugs kyi sku 'aldan don meng pa yongs su rtogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan
88a8(phal chen): 'as rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'chang chu'o// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mam pacing mangs su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub
88b1(phal chen): ma pa la ma/ sangs rgyas kyi tshan las thams ca mas ma rnams par mnganas ma mas kya pa 'ag sa thu
88b2(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos yongs su rdzogs pa tshad med pa bsam gyis ma khyab bo// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'ang sa ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi
88b3(phal chen): mkhas pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos thams cad byin gyis brlabs pa med cing spros pa thams cad med par yang thugs su chung la dge ba'i sgoms
88b4(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyang shin tu ston cing brjod de// 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas thas mkhas pa dang po'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnam
88b5(phal chen): ni chos thams cad la gzigs pa med cing / phan tshun du mkhyen pa med do// ma cings ma grol ba dang / bzung ba med cing bsags pa med de/ yongs su rdzogs pa med par yang
88b6(phal chen): thugs su chung la sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la mnga' dam pa yang brnyes te/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams chos thams cad la mnga' sbyar ba de yang yang dag pa de kho na nyid
88b7(phal chen): ma nor ba rnam pa gzhan du mi 'gyur ba dang / chos thams cad bdag gi med cing / yongs su 'dzin lha de la de kho na nyid kyi mtha' las rnam par mi 'da' yang / sangs rgyas pa
88b8(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams ni mnga' chen pos chos kyi dbyings thams cad snang ba la'ang rab tu mkhyen pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa
89a1(phal chen): gnyis pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mtshan ma'i mtha' thams cad mi mnga' ste/ mtshan mthams cad dang mi 'grogs shing / mtshan nam
89a2(phal chen): mngon par shes pa thams cad dang ma 'dres la de'i rang bzhin du ngo bo nyid med pa dang / ji ltar ngo bo med pa'i sgra'i tshul thams cad thugs su chud kyang gzugs kyi mtshan ma'i
89a3(phal chen): gzugs rnam par dag par grangs med pa dang / zhing gi mtshan ma dang / rnam par spyod pa'i mtshan ma par mi shes pa rnam pa sna tshogs yang dag par bstan cing bshang ba'i ye shes
89a4(phal chen): kyi phung po mun pa med pa 'gro ba thams cad kyi sgron ma chen por gyur pas mun pa med pa'i snang ba ston pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas
89a5(phal chen): pa gsum pa'o// chags pa med pa'i mtha' ni sngon gyi ma yid ma yin/ phyi ma'i mtha' yang ma yin/ da ltar byung ba yang ma yin te/ chos kyi dbyings su gnas pa ni 'das
89a6(phal chen): pa 'am ma 'ongs pa 'am/ nga ltar byung ba yang ma yin pas de bzhin nyid kyi mtshan nyid kyis 'byung ba med kyang sangs rgyas 'byung ba rnams kyi rigs tshad med pa'i phyir shin du
89a7(phal chen): bstan pa brjod du meng pas 'das pa dang / mabyon pa dang / nga ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas sgrub yang rab tu brjo tsang kun du gzigs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi yul gyis de bzhin
89a8(phal chen): gzigs pa 'ang ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs ma'am pa bzhi pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sgra'i 'grem las dang /
89b1(phal chen): gsung gi 'phrin las dang thugs kyi 'phrin las kyis mngon par 'du mdzad pa'ang mo mnga' la/ yongs su blang ba mi mnga' bas bzhugs shing / rnam par bya ba med pa'i mtha
89b2(phal chen): thug pa ste/ dor ba med pa'i chos kyi gnas kyi pha rol tu phyin la/ bgrang ba'i tshul las rnam par 'das kyang / tshul nges pa med pa'i mdzod du gyur cing / bgrang ba dang mngo
89b3(phal chen): par sgrub pa mtha' yas pa dang / 'jig rten pa dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa rnam pa sna tshogs tha dad pa'i grangs kyi tshul thugs su chud pa/ ye shes bsgribs pa med
89b4(phal chen): pa med pas gzigs pa rnams te/ chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi sems can gdul ba rnam par dmigs pa la rdzu 'phrul sna tshogs tshad med mu med par mngon
89b5(phal chen): par sgrub mdzad pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa lnga pa'o// chos thams cad lta ba med pas tha mi dad pa dang / bye brag me
89b6(phal chen): ba 'byung ba me pa dang / mtshan me dmang ba dang / snga tshogs med pa dang / thang ba med ma dang / dor ba med pa dang / rang bzhin mang par ba dum khyen kyang / chos kyi
89b7(phal chen): tshunges par yang dag par sgrub cing / 'jig rten gyi tshul dang 'gal ba med pa dang / rang bzhin med par yang dag par gzigs pas thams cad mkhyen pa thams cad gzigs pa
89b8(phal chen): mkhyen par bya ba rnams cad ma lus par gzigs pas chos la mnga' byur pa thams cad kyang rab tu ston la/ de bzhin cad kyi rang banan las kyang mi rnam pa 'dzi tshe sangs rgyas
90a1(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thabs mkhas pa drug pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni thugs su chud pa'i rnam pa gcig gis gzhan dang gzhan
90a2(phal chen): mkhyen par bya ba chos de'i skyon med pa las rnam par ma 'das pa/ gnas med pa dge ba'i rtsa ba'i rnam par dag pa/ mnyam pa nyid kyi chos skyon med pa gcig gis
90a3(phal chen): gzhan dus thams cad du gnas pa rab tu mkhyen te/ de la yang nyi ma gcig gam/ zla ba phyed dam/ lo gcig gam/ lo brgya 'am/ bskal pa 'jig pa dang / 'du bas
90a4(phal chen): rjes su brlag pa dang / phyir phyogs pa mi mnga' bar dus tshad med pa dang / nyi ma gcig dang / yud tsam gcig gi dus dang / snga dro nas nyi ma phyed pa'i dus dang / phyi dro nas
90a5(phal chen): snga dro'i dus dang / nyi mgung nas phyi dro'i dus dang / nyi ma bgrangs pa'i dus dang / nyi ma bdun dang / zla ba phyed kyi dus dang / zla ba dang / lo dang / lo brgya'i dus dang /
90a6(phal chen): bskal ba gcig gi dus dang / tshad med grangs med bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i dus na/ phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i dus su chos bstan pa dang / chos kyi 'a
90a7(phal chen): la thags pa med cing phyir mi ldag/ rgyun chad par mi 'gyur/ bral bar mi 'gyur bar chad par mi 'gyur/ med par mi 'gyur 'jig par mi 'gyur/ sa
90a8(phal chen): bar mi 'gyur ring du mo 'gyur 'khor den gnas pa nyid du yang rgyun 'chang 'gyur te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabasams
90b1(phal chen): pa bdun pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad dunag tu dus las bab par bzhug sa pas/ sangs rgyas bcom
90b2(phal chen): 'das rnams ni mi 'jigs pa tshad med pa mnga'o// tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa/ grangs meng ba mnga' ba'o// tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa tshad med pa mnga'
90b3(phal chen): ba'o// thadad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa zad mi shes pa mnga' bo// tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa mthar thog pa med pa mnga' ba'o// thadad pa yang dag par mkhyen
90b4(phal chen): pa mtha' yas pa mnga' ba'o// thun mongs ma yin pa'i tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa mnga' ba'o// thadad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa mthar thugs pa med pa
90b5(phal chen): mnga' ba'o// tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa de kho na nyid dang ldan pa mnga' ba'o// tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa'i tshig gi tshul thams cad rab tu rtogs mnga'
90b6(phal chen): ba'o// chos thams cad tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa mnga' ba'o// bsam pa dang mos pa dang bdabang po ji lta ba bzhin du chos kyi tshul dang / rnam grangs tshul
90b7(phal chen): ji ltar rnam par bkod pa bzhin dus mtshams med par ston te/ mdo sde bye ba khrag khrig brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa rnams mdo sde de dang de la thog ma
90b8(phal chen): ma dang dbus kyi tshul gyis yang dag par ston te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa brgyad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom
91a1(phal chen): / ldan 'das rnams ni ming med kyang ming dang rigs su 'byung ba'i chos thams cad tshig dang yig gis shin du dbyangs pa'i dbyings mngon par sangs rgyas pa ste/
91a2(phal chen): ming 'das pa ma yin pa dang / ming ma 'ongs pa ma yin pa dang / ming da ltar byung ba ma yin pa dang / ming sems can ma yin pa dang / ming zhing ma yin pa dang / ming chos ma
91a3(phal chen): yin pa dang / ming yon tan ma yin pa dang / ming byang chub sems dpa' ma yin pa dang / ming sangs rgyas ma yin pa dang / ming grangs ma yin pa dang / ming grangs med pa
91a4(phal chen): ma yin pa dang / ming skye ba ma yin pa dang / ming 'gag pa ma yin pa dang / ming med pa ma yin pa dang / ming yod pa ma yin pa dang / ming gcig pa ma yin pa dang / ming
91a5(phal chen): dad pa ma yin pa dang / ming thams cad ma yin pa dang / chos thams cad rang bzhin gyis brjod du med pa dang / phyogs med pa dang / brda med pa dang / tshig gi lam ma
91a6(phal chen): pa/ sgra dang bral ba/ sgra'i rnam pa thams cad mi 'byung ba/ yongs su bsgrubs pa med pa/ byas pa dang / rnam par byas pa med pa/ rnam pa gcig pa ma yin pa/ rnam pa
91a7(phal chen): mang po ma yin pa'ang thugs su chud la/ brjod pa dang srung pa thams cad la yang pha rol du phyin pa'i mchog brnyes pa dag ste/ rnam par rtogs pa'i yul mi mnga' ba dag
91a8(phal chen): mngon par 'du mdzad pa med pa la rab tu brtson pa dag go// tshogs pa dang kun du rtogs pa dang / yongs su rtogs pa 'gags pa dag go// gyud pa thams cad la ma
91b1(phal chen): gnas par spyod pa dag ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa dgu pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
91b2(phal chen): chos thams cad kyi gzugs ma skyes pa rab tu mkhyen pa ste/ tshor ba'i spros pa med pa dang / 'du shes kyi grangs med pa dang / 'du byed kun du rgyud pa dang / rnam par
91b3(phal chen): shes pa nye bar len pa med pa dang / rang bzhin gyis nam mkha' lta bu dang / chos thams cad dben pa dang / las med pa dang / rnam par smin pa med pa dang / spyong bas
91b4(phal chen): 'byung ba med pa dang / ma grub pa dang / ma byung ba dang / grangs kyis mi brjod pa dang / yod pa ma yin pa dang / med pa ma yin pa dang / ma skyes pa dang / ma 'gags
91b5(phal chen): pa dang / kun nas nyon mongs pa med pa dang / rnam par byang ba med pa dang / skyon med pa dang / gnas med pa dang / yongs su gnas pa med pa dang / yongs su smin
91b6(phal chen): par byas pa med pa dang / rnam par btul ba med pa dang / sems can med pa dang / sems can med pa ma yin pa dang / srog med pa dang / srog med pa ma yin
91b7(phal chen): pa dang / rkyen med pa dang / rkyen med pa ma yin pa dang / rten med pa dang / rkye rten pa med pa ma yin par chos thams cad thugs su chud kyang / chos kyi dbyings
91b8(phal chen): thams cad shin du bstan pa la pha rol tu phyin pa'i dam pa brnyes pa dag ste/ nges pa dang / ma nges pa dang log par nges pa'i phung gsum rnam par dgod pa rnams la
92a1(phal chen): stobs bcus thugs su chud pa'i ye shes mi 'jigs pa bzhis rnam par dag pa'i sangs rgyas kyi yul chen po dang ldan pas seng ge'i sgra spogs pa 'di ni sangs
92a2(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa bcu ste// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mthabs mkhas pal/

110b8(phal chen): gi rgyung ngu gtogs pa thams cad dang phyogs kyi dra ba dang rgyud 'byam klas pa ma lus pa thams cad la mi gnas pa/ brtan zhing mi g.yo la nyams pa med pa'i ye shes
111a1(phal chen): kyis rab tu gamigs pa/ chos ma lus pa thams cad kyi macang thug pa/ ga thamams cad mangs su yang ba/ drugs rnam par thal zhing dag pa ma mnga' 'das
111a2(phal chen): shes rab rnam par grol bas shin du rnam par grol ba/ yang dag pa'i mtha' mi zang pas klas pa/ chags pa med par rnam par spyod pa/ rtag tu mnyam par bzhag pa/ dus
111a3(phal chen): gsum thams cad du bsgribs pa med par 'byung ba/ sems can thams cad kyi dus gsum gyi sems dang spyod pa thams cad ma lus par thugs ska cig gis rab tu mkhyen pa
111a4(phal chen): ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi spyong pa rgyal mtshan gyi rnamachos brgyad da'o// gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan
111a5(phal chen): nams kyi chos kyi sku ni sku mnga' ba ste/ rang bzhin gcig tu gyur pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi yul tshad med pa'i sku'o// mtha' dang dpung med par yongs su grub pa'i sgra'o//
111a6(phal chen): 'jig rten thams cad kyis zad par mi nus pa'i sku'o// khams gsum pas gos pa med pa'i sku'o// brten pa'i sras rnam par dmigs pa'o// lug pa'i bsam pa dang
111a7(phal chen): rjes su dran pa'i byin gyi rlabs kyis su'i rang bzhin yang dag par ston pa'o// bden pa med pa dang 'thun pa med pa'i sku mnyam pa nyid kyis yongs su dag pa'o// chos
111a8(phal chen): bzung ba parang byon pa med pa'i grum// 'dus ma byam pas 'dzig pa med pa'i sgra'o// mtshan cing med pas mtshan cing bcis tsha'i rgyas kyi su'i ring ba mam/ yu ma ma ni/
111b1(phal chen): pa dang / byags nam 'das pa'i skul/ mams pa mas ca kyi las can 'o/ sangs rgyas rnam / sa d+ha rna @
111b2(phal chen): bzhin no// lus thams cad du yongs su gzhol ba'i sku sna tshogs su rnam par dmigs pa mdzad kyang chos kyi sku'i tshul gyi rjes su 'brang ba'o// ye shes kun du snang ba'i snying
111b3(phal chen): po can no// sku yongs su kyi mdzod du gyur pa'o// chos kyi dbyings rnam par tha dad pa med pa shin tu bstan pa'i sku'o// khams ma lus pa thams cad rgyas par 'gyengs
111b4(phal chen): pas kun du khyab pa'i sku'i rang bzhin no// mi g.yo mi 'gongs pa'i sku rnam par dag pa'o// yod pa yang ma yin med pa yang ma yin pa'i tshul dang tshul ma yin par rab tu
111b5(phal chen): brjod pa'i sku'o// sems can gyi mos pa rnam par sna tshogs 'dul bar 'gyur ba'i sku'o// 'gags pa yang ma yin ma 'gags pa yang ma yin pas 'dul ba ston pa'i
111b6(phal chen): sku'o// yon tan rin po che thams cad yang dag par 'byung bas shin tu 'phags pa'i sku'o// chos thams cad sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi de bzhin nyid du yang dag par bsgrubs
111b7(phal chen): ba'i sgra'o// rang bzhin gyis rab tu ni ning bsgrubs pa med pa'i ma par rngan pa'i sku'o// gas pa ma la tsu mas rgyas chung ba'i ga'o// thams ca
111b8(phal chen): su song ba'i chos kyi dbyings kyis rnam par dag cing / 'jig rten thams cad du shin tu rnam par phye ba'i sgra'o// phyir mi ldog cing bsgribs pa mi mdze' la/ sangs rgyas kyi rnams
112a1(phal chen): ma su bang ba ya sa la sa sa byu pa sa
112a2(phal chen): pa'i ma tham sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos dkra pa'o// gzhan mang sang rgyas bcom ldan marnams kyims rnam pa mang pa da marnam pa meng ban
112a3(phal chen): mthams cad kyis rdugs sa chung bas/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thamasas kyis 'byung ba'o// mdzan pa grub pa'i grong ba kyang 'dra 'phags pa'i sman lam dang/
112a4(phal chen): chub sems dpa'i spyod pas rnam par dag pa'o// byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad kyis yongs su rdzogs par byas pa'o// tha dad pa meng ba'o// sangs rgyas thams cad
112a5(phal chen): kyi byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad byung ba'o// byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rgya mtsho'i pyod pa'i tshul thams cad thugs su chud pa'o// smon lam dang stong pa chen pos
112a6(phal chen): yongs su dag pa'o// spyod pa thams cad mi mnyam pa med pa'ang yongs su rdzogs par byas pa'o// spyod pa'i spobs mthub par dka' ba'i spyod pa thams cad kyis mngon par byung

112b1(phal chen): mams ma patsha pas kyi tshul mkhyen pa'o// 'jacha ba mamam 'a pasachos kyi cha bangs pa na ma du la
112b2(phal chen): kyi tshul ston pa mkhyen pa'o// mnyam pa med pa dang / mnyam pas shin tu dag pa'o// srung thugs dang gsung gi yan lag dag par myong ba rnams la 'dzin las gsum
112b3(phal chen): mangs su dag par dang sangs rgyas kyi bsgom pas brnyas pa'o// sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spong pas brnyes pa'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs thams cad bsgreng pa'i
112b4(phal chen): tu sangs rgyas kyi ye shes kyis mdzad pa thams cad rab tu byung ba'o// thams cad mkhyen pa'i pa'i gnas kyi bstan pa tshad meng ba'i gnas kyi rtsa ba med pa dang ldan pa'o//
112b5(phal chen): mngon par shes thams cad kyis thar thug par mi 'gyur ba'o// 'jig rten gyi sems kyis spyod pa'i shes pa thams cad kyis bsam gyis mi khyab pa'o// chos thams ca
112b6(phal chen): ma lus par mkhyen cing gzigs pas sems can thams cad yongs su slob pa'o// dus gsum yangs pa thams cad kyi tshul shin tu 'phra ba mtha' dang dbul med pa ma
112b7(phal chen): lus par mthun pa'o// 'jig rten las 'das pa'i don mkhyen pa'i phyir/ zla ba'i mags thugs su chung pas 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad rnam pa
112b8(phal chen): bdag pa/ phyir mi ldog pa'i legs kyis sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las brjod du med pa 'jig rten thams cad du sbyor ba'o// sangs rgyas kyi sku bgrangs pa thams cad
113a1(phal chen): thugasas chung ba'i gams kyis mag me pa tshas gas na pal/ ma ma tshag sa rnam par bya mas tham ga brdu pa mtshan pa
113a2(phal chen): brjod du med pa thugs su chud pa'o// kun tu bzang po'i ye shes kyis dge ba'i chos spyad pa thams cad rnam par dag pa'o// dam bcas pa'i tshul bzhin du sems can thams/
113a3(phal chen): cad kyi lus dang skye mched ji lta bar thugs skad cig dang ldan pa'i shes rab kyis chos thams cad khong du chud bar ston pa mkhyen pa'o// chos thams cad kyi don du chos yongs su ba
113a4(phal chen): zhing rim mor bya bas thugs sa chud pa'o// 'jig can gyi khams thams cad ma lus par yul du gyur ba'o// chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad yul du gyur pa'o// dum sas

113b1(phal chen): rnam pa thams cad la mu med pa'o// dus gsum gyi rnam pa thams cad la mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas kyi lha mchog gi mad+ma phyung ba'i rnam pa thams cad la chang med pa
113b2(phal chen): mas shes bya'i rnam pa thags cad la lhag ma ma lus pa ste/ de dag thams cad lhag ma med par mngon par sangs rgyas pas sangs rgyas kyi ye shes sangs rgyas kyi rdzu 'phrul dang rnam
113b3(phal chen): par 'phrul pas 'byung ba thams cad thugs su chud pa dang / mkhyen pa thams cad rgyun chad pa med de/ de la sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sangs rgyas kyi khyu mchog
113b4(phal chen): mthu phyung ba'i skas mtha' dang dbus med par spyod pa yin/ chags pa med pa'i thugs kyis myong ba mtha' dang dbus med par spyod pa yin/ thugs rjes chen po'i sbyor
113b5(phal chen): bas dus thams cad du rtag tu rkun mi 'chad par chos bstan pa la spyod pas/ mtha' dang dbus med par spyod pa yin te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
113b6(phal chen): kyi sangs rgyas kyi mthun po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi byung ba'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos bcu pa ma/ kye rgyal ba'i mas ngag brgyab re mi sangs rgyas bcom ldan
113b7(phal chen): 'das rnams kyi mthu po che chen po'i stabs sangs rgyas kyi myong pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos rnams te/ 'das dang ma 'ongs pa dang nga ltar byung ba'i sems can thams cad
113b8(phal chen): dang / nyam thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi bsam gyis mi khyab cing dpag tu med pa dag go// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
114a1(phal chen): rnams kyi tshogs pa mamanga' ba rnams te/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das mi dga' ldan gyi mang sring bar bzugs nas 'gro ba la chags pa /
114a2(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni zla ba bcas lham pa bstan pa la thags pa mi mnga'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mngon par 'byung bar dgyes pa
114a3(phal chen): thugs kyis mngon par 'byung ba la thogs pa ma mnga'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams na drung chub kyi gang drung ngu bzhugs rnam sangs rgyas kyi tshas thams cad man
